| 0:21:23| The police dispatchers don't work for the police department. | 1:18:33| So CIT, it stands for Crisis Intervention Team.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4713)|
| 1:18:34| And that's the entire premise behind CIT is it takes a team.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4714)|
| 1:18:43| So it was actually developed in 1987 in the city of Memphis.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4723)|
| 1:18:47| They had an incident with an individual that was suffering from mental illness.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4727)|
| 1:18:50| He was in crisis.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4730)|
| 1:18:51| Police got involved, unfortunately ended up having to use deadly force.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4731)|
| 1:18:56| And so the community came together and said, hey, how can we address mental health in the| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4736)|
| 1:19:00| city?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4740)|
| 1:19:01| So there were a few people that worked together.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4741)|
| 1:19:03| The mayor of Memphis worked with NAMI, worked with the police, with mental health professionals.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4743)|
| 1:19:08| And they started the CIT program in Memphis.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4748)|
| 1:19:11| We got it here in Knoxville.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4751)|
| 1:19:12| I believe Captain Jones and Candace Allen from Home Runs McNabb attended their first| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4752)|
| 1:19:17| training in 2011 and then actually conducted the first training for KPD in 2012.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4757)|
| 1:19:23| So what CIT is, it's a community response to people who are experiencing some sort of| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4763)|
| 1:19:30| crisis.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4770)|
| 1:19:31| It doesn't have to be a mental health crisis, but a lot of times it is.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4771)|
| 1:19:34| And so what happens is you have agencies that work together to try to address those issues.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4774)|
| 1:19:42| So currently we have a regional CIT board that's comprised of Helen Ross McNabb, KPD,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4782)|
| 1:19:47| KPSO, AAR is coming back to the table.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4787)|
| 1:19:50| You have the University of Tennessee Medical Center.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4790)|
| 1:19:53| We train both security and actually the emergency department staff at UT to handle these situations.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4793)|
| 1:20:03| We've also trained Blount County Alcoa PD.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4803)|
| 1:20:06| So it's an outreach of several different agencies and partners in the community to try to address| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4806)|
| 1:20:12| the mental health issues that we see in our community.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4812)|
| 1:20:14| So we train the recruits through the core curriculum training.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4814)|
| 1:20:17| Like I said, we train other agencies.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4817)|

| 1:21:00| was what if you had someone CIT trained to answer the 911 call.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4860)|
| 1:21:05| So you have a dispatcher that's trained in CIT.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4865)|
| 1:21:09| You have the police who respond who are trained in CIT.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4869)|
| 1:21:12| You have AMR who responds who's trained in CIT.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4872)|
| 1:21:15| And then when you get them to the hospital, you have the nursing staff and you actually| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4875)|
| 1:21:19| have the security.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4879)|

| 1:21:23| Everybody's working with the same de-escalation and verbal skills.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4883)|
| 1:21:26| We're all on the same page because what we would see sometimes is we would have one of| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4886)|
| 1:21:30| those parties interact with a consumer, de-escalate the situation, then you would have someone| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4890)|
| 1:21:35| who was not CIT trained come to the scene and it would actually kind of start to fall| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4895)|
| 1:21:40| apart because we weren't on the same page about how to address the consumers.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4900)|
| 1:21:45| So CIT is really a community approach.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4905)|
| 1:21:48| It's a multi-agency approach and it's all about the partnerships and how we work together.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4908)|
| 1:21:52| So that's what we do here at KPD.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4912)|
| 1:21:55| Like I said, all of our officers went through in-service and got the core curriculum, the| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4915)|
| 1:21:59| three-day curriculum in 2018.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4919)|
| 1:22:01| All of our current recruit classes get the core curriculum when they go through.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4921)|
| 1:22:07| And then officers can then apply to join the actual CIT team once they're out of the academy,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4927)|
| 1:22:13| which is the full 40-hour course.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4933)|
| 1:22:16| And we usually do two of those schools in a given calendar year.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4936)|
| 1:22:20| So that's something if an officer chooses to receive that additional training for the| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4940)|
| 1:22:24| 40 hours, then they can do so.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-ws-r-3877-200723?start=4944)|
